value="65"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>subprocess<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> module supports three APIs for working with</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="66"></td><td class="line-content">processes. The <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>run()<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> function, added in Python 3.5, is a</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="67"></td><td class="line-content">high-level API for running a process and optionally collecting its</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="68"></td><td class="line-content">output. The functions <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>call()<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>check_call()<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span>, and</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="69"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>check_output()<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> are the former high-level API, carried over from</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="70"></td><td class="line-content">Python 2. They are still supported and widely used in existing</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="71"></td><td class="line-content">programs. The class <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>Popen<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> is a low-level API used to build</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="72"></td><td class="line-content">the other APIs and useful for more complex process interactions. The</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="73"></td><td class="line-content">constructor for <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>Popen<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/code&gt;</span> takes arguments to set up the new</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="74"></td><td class="line-content">process so the parent can communicate with it via pipes.  It provides</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="75"></td><td class="line-content">all of the functionality of the other modules and functions it</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="76"></td><td class="line-content">replaces, and more. The API is consistent for all uses, and many of</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="77"></td><td class="line-content">the extra steps of overhead needed (such as closing extra file</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="78"></td><td class="line-content">descriptors and ensuring the pipes are closed) are “built in” instead</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="79"></td><td class="line-content">of being handled by the application code separately.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="80"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The <span class="html-tag">&lt;code <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">docutils literal notranslate</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">pre</span>"&gt;</span>subprocess<span
